Tips for getting started:
1. Ask questions, edit files, or run commands.
2. Be specific for the best results.
3. Create GEMINI.md files to customize your interactions with Gemini.
4. /help for more information.

Tips for getting started:
1. Ask questions, edit files, or run commands.
2. Be specific for the best results.
3. Create GEMINI.md files to customize your interactions with Gemini.
4. /help for more information.

Tips for getting started:
1. Ask questions, edit files, or run commands.
2. Be specific for the best results.
3. Create GEMINI.md files to customize your interactions with Gemini.
4. /help for more information.

Tips for getting started:
1. Ask questions, edit files, or run commands.
2. Be specific for the best results.
3. Create GEMINI.md files to customize your interactions with Gemini.
4. /help for more information.

  compte le repertoire V0.

â ´ Defining Next Steps (esc to cancel, 6s)



~/study/git/monShell          no sandbox (see   gemini-2.5-pro (99%
(fonction_executer*)          /docs)           context left)

[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[1A[2K[G
    1     #include <stdio.h>
    2     #include <stdlib.h>
    3     #include <unistd.h>
    4     #include <sys/types.h>
    5     #include <sys/wait.h>
    6
    7     enum {
    8         MaxPathLength = 512,    //
      longueur max d'un nom de fichier
    9     };
   10
   11     void executer_cmd(char **mot, char
      **dirs) {
   12         int tmp;
   13         char pathname[MaxPathLength];
   14         int i;
   15
   16         tmp = fork();     // lancer le
      processus enfant
   17
   18         if (tmp < 0) {
   19             perror("fork");
   20             return;
   21         }
   22
   23         if (tmp != 0) {
   24             while(wait(0) != tmp);
   25             return;
   26         }
   27
   28         // enfant: exec du programme
   29         for(i = 0; dirs[i] != 0; i++) {
   30             snprintf(pathname, sizeof
      pathname, "%s/%s", dirs[i], mot[0]);
   31             execv(pathname, mot);
   32         }
   33
   34         fprintf( stderr, "%s: not
      found\n", mot[0]);
   35         exit(1);
   36     }

    1     #include <stdio.h>
    2     #include <stdlib.h>
    3     #include <string.h>
    4     #include <unistd.h>
    5
    6     #include "executer.h"
    7
    8     enum {
    9         MaxLigne = 1024,        //
      longueur max d'une ligne de commande
   10         MaxMot = MaxLigne / 2,  // nbre
      max de mot dans la ligne
   11         MaxDirs = 100,          // nbre
      max de repertoire dans PATH
   12     };
   13
   14     void decouper(char *, char *, char
      **, int);
   15
   16     #define PROMPT "? "
   17
   18     int main (int argc, char * argv[]) {
   19
   20         char ligne[MaxLigne];
   21         char * mot[MaxMot];
   22         char * dirs[MaxDirs];
   23
   24         /* Decouper une partie de PATH en
      repertoires */
   25         decouper(strdup(getenv("PATH")),
      ":",dirs, MaxDirs);
   26
   27         /* Lire et traiter chaque ligne
      de commande */
   28         for (
   29             printf(PROMPT);
   30             fgets(ligne, sizeof ligne,
      stdin) != 0;
   31             printf(PROMPT) ) {
   32
   33             decouper(ligne, " \t\n", mot,
      MaxMot);
   34
   35             if (mot[0] == 0)  // ligne
      vide
   36                 continue;
   37
   38             executer_cmd(mot, dirs);
   39         }
   40
   41         printf("Bye\n");
   42         return 0;
   43     }
